        for(var x = 1; x < array.length-1; x+=2){
            if(array[x].indexOf('cat') > -1){
                parsedUrl += array[x+1] + '|'
            }

        }
        parsedUrl = 'browse:' + parsedUrl;
        return parsedUrl.toLowerCase().substring(0,parsedUrl.length-1);
    }

  ga('create', 'UA-3403544-1', 'auto');
  ga('require', 'displayfeatures');
  ga('send', 'pageview');

  // Scroll tracking script
  jQuery(function($) {
    // Debug flag
    var debugMode = false;

    // Default time delay before checking location
    var callBackTime = 100;

    // # px before tracking a reader
    var readerLocation = 150;

    // Set some flags for tracking & execution
    var timer = 0;
    var scroller = false;
    var endContent = false;
    var didComplete = false;

    // Set some time variables to calculate reading time
    var startTime = new Date();
    var beginning = startTime.getTime();
    var totalTime = 0;
    
    // Get some information about the current page
    var pageTitle = document.title;

    // Track the aticle load
    if (!debugMode) {
        ga('send', 'event', 'Reading', 'ArticleLoaded', pageTitle, {'nonInteraction': 1});
    } else {
        alert('The page has loaded. Woohoo.');    
    }

    // Check the location and track user
    function trackLocation() {
        bottom = $(window).height() + $(window).scrollTop();
        height = $(document).height();

        // If user starts to scroll send an event
        if (bottom > readerLocation && !scroller) {
            currentTime = new Date();
            scrollStart = currentTime.getTime();
            timeToScroll = Math.round((scrollStart - beginning) / 1000);
            if (!debugMode) {
                ga('send', 'event', 'Reading', 'StartReading', pageTitle, timeToScroll, {'metric1' : timeToScroll});
            } else {
                alert('started reading ' + timeToScroll);
            }
            scroller = true;
        }

        // If user has hit the bottom of the content send an event
        if (bottom >= $('#store-content').scrollTop() + $('#store-content').innerHeight() && !endContent) {
            currentTime = new Date();
            contentScrollEnd = currentTime.getTime();
            timeToContentEnd = Math.round((contentScrollEnd - scrollStart) / 1000);
            if (!debugMode) {
                 if (timeToContentEnd < 60) {
                    ga('set', 'dimension5', 'Scanner'); 
                } else {
                    ga('set', 'dimension5', 'Reader'); 
                }
                ga('send', 'event', 'Reading', 'ContentBottom', pageTitle, timeToContentEnd, {'metric2' : timeToContentEnd});
            } else {
                alert('end content section '+timeToContentEnd);
            }
            endContent = true;
        }

        // If user has hit the bottom of page send an event
        if (bottom >= height && !didComplete) {
            currentTime = new Date();
            end = currentTime.getTime();
            totalTime = Math.round((end - scrollStart) / 1000);
            if (!debugMode) {
                ga('send', 'event', 'Reading', 'PageBottom', pageTitle, totalTime, {'metric3' : totalTime});
            } else {
                alert('bottom of page '+totalTime);
            }
            didComplete = true;
        }
    }

    // Track the scrolling and track location
    $(window).scroll(function() {
        if (timer) {
            clearTimeout(timer);
        }

        // Use a buffer so we don't call trackLocation too often.
        timer = setTimeout(trackLocation, callBackTime);
    });
});
 
</script>

       <h1>Tracking Numbers</h1> 
       <p>Your shipping confirmation email will contain a tracking number for the carrier used to ship your order. Visit the carrier's website and enter the tracking number to check your package's progress.</p> 
       <p>Registered customers can check order status and access tracking numbers in their <a href="https://www.swansonvitamins.com/my-account/order-history.html">Order History</a>.</p>
       <div id="help-faq"> 
        <h2>Frequently Asked Questions</h2> 
        <h3>How long will it take to get my order with standard shipping?</h3> 
        <p>Our standard shipping time frame is 4 to 6 business days from the date your order ships. We normally allow 48 business hours to process your order, although this can change based on order volume.</p>
       </div>

   <script type="text/javascript">
	$(document).ready(function(){
		$('#email-sign-footer').submit(function (e) {
			var emailFtr1 = $('#shpFtrEmailAddress2').val();

			$('#shpFtrEmailAddressConfirm').val(emailFtr1);
			sendAjaxFtrEmail();
			return false;
		});
	})
	function sendAjaxFtrEmail() {
		var fie1       = '#shpFtrEmailAddress2';
		var fie2       = '#shpFtrEmailAddressConfirm';
		var emField    = $.trim($(fie1).val());
		var conEmField = $.trim($(fie2).val());
		var flag       = 0;

		// set error styles
		function errorCol(field) {
			$(field).css({background: "#ecadad", border: "1px solid #d78282"});
		}

		// reset default styles
		function defaultCol(field) {
			$(field).css({background: "#ffffff", border: "1px solid #cfcfcf"});
		}

		// visual feedback on validation
		if (emField == '' || emField == null || emField == "Enter your email address") {
			errorCol(fie1);
		} else {
			defaultCol(fie1);
			if (shp_validate.email(emField)) {
				if (emField === conEmField) {
					defaultCol(fie1);
					defaultCol(fie2);
					flag = 1;
				} else {
					errorCol(fie2);
				}
			} else {
				errorCol(fie1);
			}
		}

		// send data & respond
		if (flag == 1) {
			var postData = $("#email-sign-footer").serializeArray();
			$('#email-signup-form').attr('data-location', 'Chronic Footer Signup');
			$.ajax({
				url: "/emailsignup.json",
				type: 'POST',
				data: postData,
				success: function (data) {
					if (data.signup == 'success') {
						$('#email-sign-footer').addClass('first-signup');
					} else {
						$('#email-sign-footer').addClass('return-signup');
					}
					if ($(".first-signup").length > 0) {
						$("#emailConfirmSuccessFooter").removeClass('hidden').fadeIn(800);
						$("#footerEmailSignUp").addClass('hidden');
					} else if ($(".return-signup").length > 0) {
						$.cookie('email-signup_shown', "true", {expires: 365, path: '/'});
						$("#emailAlreadyFooter").removeClass('hidden').fadeIn(800);
						$("#footerEmailSignUp").addClass('hidden');
					}
				},
				error: function (e) {
					$('#footerEmailSignUp').addClass('real-error');
					$("#OopsErrorFooter").fadeIn(800);
					$("#footerEmailSignUp").delay(100000).slideUp(1800).removeClass('has-animated');
					$('.hide-me-on-signup').hide();
				}
			});
			return false;
		} else if (flag == 0) {
			return false;
		}
	}

	$(window).scroll(function () {
		if (!$.cookie('Signup_Shown')) {
			$('#footerEmailSignUp').show();
			$.cookie('Signup_Shown', "true", {
				expires: 30,
				path: '/'
			});
		}
	});
</script>

   <script>
	/*
	 ** Google Code for All Visitors Remarketing List
	 */

	var pageTypeChannel, pageProductId, pageTotalValue;
	// Switch statement to give Google their specific page type
	switch (dataLayer.pageType) {
		case "search":
			pageTypeChannel = "searchresults";
			break;
		case "browse":
			pageTypeChannel = "category";
			break;
		case "home":
			pageTypeChannel = "home";
			break;
		case "product":
			pageTypeChannel = "product";
			break;
		case "cart":
			pageTypeChannel = "cart";
			break;
		case "checkout":
			pageTypeChannel = "purchase";
			break;
		default:
			pageTypeChannel = "other";
	}

	// Parse product ID's and pass them to Google
	if (dataLayer.product != '') {
		pageProductId = dataLayer.product;
	} else {
		pageProductId = "";
	}

	// Price switch between product and cart price
	if (pageTypeChannel == "product") {
		pageTotalValue = parseFloat("");
	} else if (pageTypeChannel == "cart" || pageTypeChannel == "purchase") {
		pageTotalValue = parseFloat("");
	} else {
		pageTotalValue = 0;
	}
</script>
